-- 
-- Table structure for table `tbl_bundle_subscribers`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `tbl_bundle_subscribers` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `email_id` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `firstname` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `account_number` varchar(60) NOT NULL default '',
  `reward_pin_number` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `mailing_date` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `pin_allocate_status` char(1) NOT NULL default 'N',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=57 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=57 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `tbl_city`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `tbl_city` (
  `city_id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `service_name` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `service_name_fr` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `city_name` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `country_id` int(11) default NULL,
  `rates` decimal(5,2) default '0.00',
  `preferred_rates` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL default '0.00',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`city_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=1407 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1407 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `tbl_city_corp`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `tbl_city_corp` (
  `city_id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `service_name` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `city_name` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `country_id` int(11) default NULL,
  `rates` decimal(5,2) default '0.00',
  `preferred_rates` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL default '0.00',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`city_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=954 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=954 ;

-- 
-- Table structure for table `tbl_company`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `tbl_company` (
  `company_id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `company_name` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `username` varchar(10) default NULL,
  `password` varchar(10) default NULL,
  `user_type` char(1) NOT NULL default 'U',
  `status` char(1) NOT NULL default 'I',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`company_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=3 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

-- Dumping data for table `tbl_company`

-- Table structure for table `tbl_country`

  `country_id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `country_code` varchar(20) default NULL,

  `rates` decimal(5,2) default '0.00',
  `preferred_rates` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL default '0.00',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`country_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=248 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=248 ;

-- 
-- Table structure for table `tbl_country_corp`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `tbl_country_corp` (
  `country_id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `country_code` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `country_name` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `rates` decimal(5,2) default '0.00',
  `preferred_rates` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL default '0.00',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`country_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=239 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=239 ;

-- 
-- Table structure for table `tbl_testimonial`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `tbl_testimonial` (
  `t_id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `t_desc` text NOT NULL,
  `t_name` varchar(50) NOT NULL default '',
  `t_email` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `t_city` varchar(50) NOT NULL default '',
  `t_country` varchar(50) NOT NULL default '',
  `t_language` char(3) NOT NULL default 'ENG',
  `t_date` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `t_status` char(1) NOT NULL default 'N',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`t_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=13 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=13 ;
